1942px;">     <h2 id="section816451553012" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">MapComponentController<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>地图的主要功能入口类，与地图有关的所有方法从此处接入。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1043px;">     <h3 id="section6163175355113" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable" class="firsth2">animateCamera<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section6163175355113" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>animateCamera(update: CameraUpdate, duration?: number): void</p>     <p>在指定的持续时间内以动画的形式更新相机状态。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.9.1.5.1.1" width="12%">          <p><strong>参数名</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.9.1.5.1.2" width="26.13%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.9.1.5.1.3" width="9.74%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.3.9.1.5.1.4" width="52.129999999999995%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>update</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="26.13%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-cameraupdate">CameraUpdate</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="9.74%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.129999999999995%">          <p>相机状态将要发生的变化。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>duration</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="26.13%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="9.74%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.129999999999995%">          <p>动画的持续时间，单位：ms，默认值为250，取值范围：大于0，小于等于0按照默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1449px;">     <h3 id="section972910185717" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">animateCameraStatus<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section972910185717" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>animateCameraStatus(update: CameraUpdate, duration?: number): Promise&lt;AnimateResult&gt;</p>     <p>在指定的持续时间内以动画的形式更新相机状态，并返回动画结果。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.9.1.5.1.1" width="12%">          <p><strong>参数名</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.9.1.5.1.2" width="28.52%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.9.1.5.1.3" width="7.340000000000001%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.9.1.5.1.4" width="52.14%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>update</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.52%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-cameraupdate">CameraUpdate</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.340000000000001%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.14%">          <p>相机状态将要发生的变化。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>duration</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.52%">          <p>number</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.340000000000001%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.14%">          <p>动画的持续时间，单位：ms，默认值为250，取值范围：大于0，小于等于0按照默认值处理。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.11.1.3.1.1" width="32.16%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.11.1.3.1.2" width="67.84%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.16%">          <p>Promise&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-animateresult#section18741944605">AnimateResult</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="67.84%">          <p>Promise对象，返回<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-animateresult#section18741944605">AnimateResult</a>。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-errorcode">ArkTS API错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"   <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>401</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="70%">          <p>Invalid input parameter.</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-axx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-axx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="hljs-number">1000</span>);</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1611px;">     <h3 id="section02401132134312" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">animateCameraWithMarker<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section02401132134312" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>animateCameraWithMarker(update: CameraUpdate, marker: Marker, duration: number): Promise&lt;AnimateResult&gt;</p>     <p>在指定的持续时间内以动画的形式更新相机状态，并更新指定的marker。使用Promise异步回调。相机移动过程中不能被打断，否则<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-animateresult#section18741944605">AnimateResult</a>的参数isCanceled返回值为true。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.9.1.5.1.3" width="7.35%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.9.1.5.1.4" width="52.129999999999995%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>update</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.52%">          <p><a <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.129999999999995%">          <p>相机状态将要发生的变化。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>marker</p></td>         <td width="7.470000000000001%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.959999999999994%">          <p>相机最小缩放级别，取值范围：[2, 20]。</p>          <p>传入的值大于20，最小缩放级别会取20。</p>          <p>传入的值小于2，最小缩放级别会取2。</p>          <p>在取值范围内，传入的值大于当前maxZoom，最大缩放级别和最小缩放级别都会被设置为当前传入的值。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 814px;">     <h3 id="section201759451313" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setMyLocationEnabled<i class="anchor-icon id="section1151381081514" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setZoomGesturesEnabled<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1151381081514" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setZoomGesturesEnabled(enabled: boolean): void</p>     <p>设置是否启用缩放手势。默认情况下，缩放手势处于启用状态。</p>     <ul>      <li>启用状态，用户可以使用以下手势缩放相机：       <ol>        <li>单指双击可将缩放级别提高1（放大）层级，用双指单击可将缩放级别降低1（缩小）层级。</li>        <li>双指张合，实现放大缩小。</li>        <li>单指双击实现单指缩放，第二次点时按住，然后上划缩小，或下划放大。</li>       </ol></li>      <li>禁用状态，缩放手势无效。此设置不影响缩放按钮，也不限制通过接口移动相机和相机动画。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.10.1.5.1.1" width="12%">          <p><strong>参数名</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.10.1.5.1.2" width="28.52%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.10.1.5.1.3" width="7.359999999999999%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.25.10.1.5.1.4" width="52.12%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>enabled</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="28.52%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.359999999999999%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.12%">          <ul>           <li>true：启用缩放手势</li>           <li>false：禁用缩放手势</li>          </ul>          <p>默认值为true。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-axx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-axx-c106="" _ngcontent-axx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-axx-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-axx-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-axx-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">mapController</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setZoomGesturesEnabled</span>(<span class="hljs-literal">true</span>); </li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 810px;">     <h3 id="section1039191318157" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">isZoomGesturesEnabled<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1039191318157" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span  <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 870px;">     <h3 id="section31711513156" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setScrollGesturesEnabled<i class="anchor-icon   <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 894px;">     <h3 id="section299655171811" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setRotateGesturesEnabled<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section299655171811" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list   <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 870px;">     <h3 id="section183712595910" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setTiltGesturesEnabled<i class="anchor-icon <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 870px;">     <h3 id="section4116897186" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setZoomControlsEnabled<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section4116897186" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setZoomControlsEnabled(enabled: boolean): void</p>     <p>设置是否启用缩放控制器，默认情况下，缩放控件处于启用状态。</p>     <ul>      <li>启用状态，地图上会出现一对按钮的缩放控件（用于缩放地图）。点击按钮时，会使相机放大（或缩小）一个缩放级别。</li>      <li>禁用状态，不会显示缩放控件。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 870px;">     <h3 id="section45372264188" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setGestureScaleByMapCenter<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section45372264188" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setGestureScaleByMapCenter(enabled: boolean): void</p>     <p>设置以固定屏幕中心点进行缩放功能是否可用，默认是禁用状态。</p>     <ul>      <li>启用状态，地图将以传入的固定屏幕点进行缩放。通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-mapcomponentcontroller#section159768471777">setPointToCenter</a>方法设置屏幕中心点坐标。</li>      <li>禁用状态，将以手指点击的位置为中心进行缩放。</li>     </ul>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="52.12%">          <ul>           <li>true：启用，地图将以传入的固定屏幕点进行缩放。</li>           <li>false：禁用，地图将以手指点击的位置为中心进行缩放。</li>          </ul> class="typescript prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-variable language_">this</span>.<span class="hljs-property">mapController</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setLogoAlignment</span>(mapCommon.<span class="hljs-property">LogoAlignment</span>.<span class="hljs-property">BOTTOM_START</span>);</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1026px;">     <h3 id="section115618542213" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setLogoPadding<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section115618542213" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setLogoPadding(padding: mapCommon.Padding): void</p>     <p>设置地图边界与Logo之间的间距。Logo不随横竖屏而改变，大小固定不随地图缩放变化。</p>     <ul>      <li>当您设置的任意padding值超出范围（例如：负值，或超出边界）时被认为非法，Logo位置不变化。</li>      <li>当Logo位置在左下角时left、bottom生效。</li>      <li>当Logo位置在右上角时right、top生效，以此类推。</li>     </ul>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>在调整设置地图边界与Logo之间的间距时，请避免隐藏或遮盖Logo。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setPadding<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section1820681051518" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setPadding(padding?: mapCommon.Padding): void</p>     <p>设置地图和边界的距离来定义地图的可见区域。地图图层元素将适应填充，例如，缩放控件、指南针等将被移动到适应定义的区域，相机将相对于可见区域的中心移动。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.2" width="24.55%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.3" width="6.7%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.9.1.5.1.4" width="58.29%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="10.459999999999999%">          <p>padding</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="24.55%">          <p><a id="section188905329242" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">addTraceOverlay<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section188905329242" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>addTraceOverlay(params: mapCommon.TraceOverlayParams, markers?: Array&lt;Marker&gt;): Promise&lt;TraceOverlay&gt;</p>     <p>绘制动态轨迹，支持传一组标记，标记将和轨迹一起移动。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p class="msonormal"><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.9.1.5.1.1" width="12%">          <p><strong>参数名</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.9.1.5.1.2" width="37.87%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.9.1.5.1.3" width="7.91%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.9.1.5.1.4" width="42.22%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>params</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="37.87%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section202444375510">mapCommon.TraceOverlayParams</a></p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.91%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="42.22%">          <p>动态轨迹参数。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="12%">          <p>markers</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="37.87%">          <p>Array&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-marker">Marker</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="7.91%">          <p>否</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="42.22%">          <p>动态轨迹的图片数组。</p>          <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">            <p>一组标记的位置必须相同。</p>           </div></div></div></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.11.1.3.1.1" width="32.16%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.11.1.3.1.2" width="67.84%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.16%">          <p>Promise&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-traceoverlay">TraceOverlay</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="67.84%">          <p>Promise对象，返回<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-traceoverlay">TraceOverlay</a>。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-errorcode">ArkTS API错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.14.1.3.1.1" width="30%">          <p>错误码ID</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.71.14.1.3.1.2" width="70%">          <p>错误信息</p></th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>401</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="70%">          <p>Invalid input parameter.</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="30%">          <p>1002601001</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="70%">          <p>The object to be operated does not exist.</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1723px;">     <h3 id="section123390488448" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">addArc<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section123390488448" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>addArc(params: mapCommon.MapArcParams): MapArc</p>     <p>在地图上添加一条弧线。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.0.0(12)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p class="msonormal"><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">          <p><strong>参数名</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.9.1.5.1.2" width="40%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.9.1.5.1.3" width="10%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.72.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>params</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="40%">          <p><a <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>弧线的相关属性。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder"      <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.16%">          <p>MapArc</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="67.84%">          <p>返回<a id="section11626172812525" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">on('cameraChange')<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section11626172812525" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>on(type: 'cameraChange', callback: Callback&lt;mapCommon.LatLng&gt;): void</p>     <p>监听地图相机状态变化事件。使用callback异步回调。此回调不会在动画过程中触发，而是在动画结束时触发。</p>     <p>建议使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-map-mapeventmanager#section1488710318220">MapEventManager.on(type: 'cameraChange')</a>。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本4.1.0(11)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>4.1.0(11)</p>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.91.10.1.5.1.1" width="23.25%">          <p><strong>参数名</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.91.10.1.5.1.2" width="36.33%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.91.10.1.5.1.3" width="8.99%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.91.10.1.5.1.4" width="31.430000000000003%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="23.25%">          <p>type</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.33%">          <p>string</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="8.99%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.430000000000003%">          <p>'cameraChange'：监听地图相机状态变化事件。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="23.25%">          <p>callback</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="36.33%">          <p>Callback&lt;<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section20691173773810">mapCommon.LatLng</a>&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="8.99%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="31.430000000000003%">          <p>回调函数，返回<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/map-common#section20691173773810">mapCommon.LatLng</a>，监听地图相机状态变化事件。该回调不会在动画过程中触发，而是在动画结束时触发。</p></td>        </tr> 1105px;">     <h3 id="section12159164214612" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable">setIndoorMapEnabled<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="section12159164214612" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setIndoorMapEnabled(enabled: boolean): void</p>     <p>打开或关闭室内图。仅17级及以上地图层级可见室内图，仅18级及以上地图层级可见楼层调节控件。</p>     <p><strong>模型约束：</strong>此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong>从版本5.1.1(19)开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Map.Core</p>     <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>在API19及之后版本该接口在phone、tablet、2in1均可正常使用，在其他设备中返回801错误。</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.1.1(19)</p>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.139.10.1.5.1.1" width="23.25%">          <p><strong>参数名</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.139.10.1.5.1.2" width="23.49%">          <p><strong>类型</strong></p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.139.10.1.5.1.3" width="11.86%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.139.10.1.5.1.4" width="41.4%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="23.25%">          <p>enabled</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="23.49%">          <p>boolean</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="11.86%">          <p>是</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="41.4%">          <p>是否启用室内图，默认关闭，异常值按照默认值处理。取值范围：</p>          <ul>           <li>true：启用室内图</li>           <li>false：关闭室内图</li>          </ul></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a
